     (function () {
         var getCookie = function (name) {
                 var v = document.cookie.match('(^|;) ?' + name + '=([^;]*)(;|$)');
                 return v ? v[2] : null;
             },
             optOutCookie = getCookie("SPARKASSE_GLOBAL_OPT_OUT"),
             iframe = false,
             appendIframe = function () {
                 var page='https://www.erstegroup.com/content/f696769a/-4206-4852-b577-5adda327c15c/iframe.html';
             if (!iframe){
                 iframe = document.createElement("iframe");
                 iframe.setAttribute("frameBorder","0");
                 iframe.style.display = "none";
                 iframe.src=page+(page.indexOf("?")!=-1?'&':'?')+"parentpage="+encodeURIComponent(document.location.href);
                 document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].appendChild(iframe);
             }else{
                 iframe.src=page+(page.indexOf("?")!=-1?'&':'?')+"parentpage="+encodeURIComponent(document.location.href);
             } 
             //console.log(iframe)
             };
         
         //embed iframe
             // document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){
             if(optOutCookie === null){
                 appendIframe();
             }
         //});
         //change iframe on adding or changing URL Hash
         if(window.attachEvent){
             window.attachEvent("onhashchange", function () {
                 if(optOutCookie === null) {
                     appendIframe();
                 }
             });
         } else {
             window.addEventListener("hashchange", function () {
                 if(optOutCookie === null) {
                         appendIframe();
                     }
              });
         }
       //console.log(optOutCookie) 
     }());
